// Exile's Curse (Adept) (god-pve,god-pvp)
//notes: Worthy Variant
PvE: Any + Liquid Coil + Field Prep/Grave Robber + MKC/Disruption Break
PvP: Fluted/Smallbore/Polygonal + Liquid Coils + Firmly Planted + Elemental Cap
Chosen Variant
PvE: Any + Liquid Coils + Slideshot + Vorpal/HIR
PvP: Fluted/Smallbore/Polygonal + Liquid Coils + Slideshot/Quickdraw + HIR/Kickstart
Kickstart is a nice perk to reduce the charge time slightly, but has a very small period to proc it (needs charging during slide to ensure that you don’t lose the perk half way through the burst), and requires you to play a certain way to best use the perk (sprinting with a fusion out in order to get the perk to proc, leaving you vulnerable to a shotgun push or ranged primary fire) tags:god-pve,god-pvp

// Exile's Curse (Adept) (god-pvp)

Chosen Variant
PvP: Fluted/Smallbore/Polygonal + Liquid Coils + Slideshot/Quickdraw + HIR/Kickstart
Kickstart is a nice perk to reduce the charge time slightly, but has a very small period to proc it (needs charging during slide to ensure that you don’t lose the perk half way through the burst), and requires you to play a certain way to best use the perk (sprinting with a fusion out in order to get the perk to proc, leaving you vulnerable to a shotgun push or ranged primary fire) tags:god-pvp
